import hashlib, json, datetime, csv, sys, os, random

def S_proof(beta: float, dCe: float, lamb: float):
    """Calcule S et produit une empreinte de preuve intÃ©grÃ©e"""
    S = round((beta * dCe) / (lamb if lamb != 0 else 1e-6), 6)

def test_event(description: str):

import hashlib, datetime, random

def zoran_test(phenomenon:str):
    # Extraction simplifiÃ©e (pour dÃ©mo)
    beta = round(random.uniform(0.8,1.4),2)
    dCe  = round(random.uniform(0.8,1.4),2)
    lamb = round(random.uniform(0.8,1.4),2)
    S = round((beta*dCe)/lamb,2)

    if S > 1.1: verdict = "regen"
    elif S < 0.9: verdict = "desordre"
    else: verdict = "stable"

    report = {
        "phenomenon": phenomenon,
        "Î²": beta, "Î”Câ‚‘": dCe, "Î»": lamb, "S": S,
        "verdict": verdict,
        "timestamp": datetime.datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
    }
    # Hash de preuve
    h = hashlib.sha512(str(report).encode()).hexdigest()
    report["SHA512i"] = h
    return report

# Exemple d'utilisation

ğŸ§  Zoran Atlas Tester â€” prototype local

#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Zoran Atlas Tester  â€“  Prototype local
-------------------------------------
Lit une description de phÃ©nomÃ¨ne, calcule S = (Î²Â·Î”Câ‚‘)/Î»,
interprÃ¨te le rÃ©sultat (regen / stable / dÃ©sordre),
et Ã©crit un rapport horodatÃ© avec empreinte SHA-512.
Usage :
    python zoran_atlas_tester.py "Description du phÃ©nomÃ¨ne"
"""

import hashlib, datetime, csv, random, sys, os, json

def zoran_test(phenomenon:str):
    beta = round(random.uniform(0.8, 1.4), 3)
    dCe  = round(random.uniform(0.8, 1.4), 3)
    lamb = round(random.uniform(0.8, 1.4), 3)
    S = round((beta * dCe) / lamb, 3)

    if S > 1.1:
        verdict = "regen"
    elif S < 0.9:
        verdict = "desordre"
    else:
        verdict = "stable"

    report = {
        "phenomenon": phenomenon,
        "Î²": beta,
        "Î”Câ‚‘": dCe,
        "Î»": lamb,
        "S": S,
        "verdict": verdict,
        "timestamp": datetime.datetime.utcnow().isoformat()+"Z"
    }

    # empreinte de preuve
    report["SHA512i"] = hashlib.sha512(json.dumps(report).encode()).hexdigest()
    return report

def save_report(report, path="Atlas_results.csv"):
    exists = os.path.isfile(path)
    with open(path, "a", newline="", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        writer = csv.DictWriter(f, fieldnames=report.keys())
        if not exists:
            writer.writeheader()
        writer.writerow(report)
    print(f"[âœ“] Rapport ajoutÃ© â†’ {path}")

def main():
    if len(sys.argv) < 2:
        print(__doc__)
        sys.exit(0)
    phenomenon = " ".join(sys.argv[1:])
    r = zoran_test(phenomenon)
    print(json.dumps(r, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False))
    save_report(r)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

# donnÃ©es figÃ©es
PREDICTIONS = [
    (1, "Physique", "Couplage gravito-quantique Ã  tempÃ©rature ambiante (Î”Câ‚‘>1)",
     "Observation expÃ©rimentale dâ€™un effet de couplage gravito-quantique mesurÃ© Ã  T>250 K"),

     "Publication dÃ©crivant une mÃ©thode de rÃ©gÃ©nÃ©ration cellulaire non gÃ©nique (+20 % longÃ©vitÃ© in vitro)"),

     "Annonce dâ€™un LLM dotÃ© dâ€™un systÃ¨me dâ€™auto-alignement interne mesurable"),

def hash_record(record: dict) -> str:
    """retourne empreinte SHA-512i dâ€™un dictionnaire"""
    payload = json.dumps(record, sort_keys=True).encode("utf-8")
    return hashlib.sha512(payload).hexdigest()

def main():

    out_csv = "Predictions_2025.csv"
    out_hash = "Predictions_2025_SHA512i.txt"

    rows = []
    for id_, dom, desc, falsif in PREDICTIONS:

            "id": id_,
            "domaine": dom,
            "description": desc,
            "falsifiable": falsif,

    with open(out_csv, "w", newline="", encoding="utf-8") as f:

        writer.writeheader()

    # empreinte globale du fichier CSV

    print(f"[âœ“] Fichier crÃ©Ã© : {out_csv}")
